- BorderOuterV
- Drag from window menu button (upper-left button) to undock an entire node (all windows).
- Drag from window title bar or their tab to dock/undock.
- Hold SHIFT to disable docking.
- If you need to add/remove fonts at runtime (e.g. for DPI change), do it before calling NewFrame().
- ImGuiTableFlags_SizingFixedFit if ScrollX is on or if host window has ImGuiWindowFlags_AlwaysAutoResize.
- ImGuiTableFlags_SizingStretchSame otherwise.
- Load additional fonts with io.Fonts->AddFontFromFileTTF().
- OuterSize.x < 0.0f will right-align the table.
- OuterSize.x = 0.0f will narrow fit the table unless there are any Stretch column.
- OuterSize.y then becomes the minimum size for the table, which will extend vertically if there are more rows (unless NoHostExtendY is set).
- Read FAQ and docs/FONTS.md for more details.
- The font atlas is built when calling io.Fonts->GetTexDataAsXXXX() or io.Fonts->Build().
- The table is output directly in the parent window.
- any form of row selection
- or me
- to position popup/tooltips so they don't straddle monitors.
- to query DPI settings on a per monitor basis

By Omar Cornut and all Dear ImGui contributors.
By default, Selectables uses style.SelectableTextAlign but it can be overridden on a per-item basis using PushStyleVar(). You'll probably want to always keep your default situation to left-align otherwise it becomes difficult to layout multiple items on a same line
By default, anti-aliased lines are turned OFF.
By default, colors are given to ColorEdit and ColorPicker in RGB, but ImGuiColorEditFlags_InputHSVallows you to store colors as HSV and pass them to ColorEdit and ColorPicker as HSV. This comes with theadded benefit that you can manipulate hue values with the picker even when saturation or value are zero.
By default, labels are in UTC time but can be set to use local time instead.
By default, right-clicking over a TableHeadersRow()/TableHeader() line will open the default context-menu.

When ImPlotAxisFlags_Time is enabled on the X-Axis, values are interpreted as
When ScrollX is enabled, the default sizing policy becomes ImGuiTableFlags_SizingFixedFit, as automatically stretching columns doesn't make much sense with horizontal scrolling.
When a popup is active, it inhibits interacting with windows that are behind the popup. Clicking outside the popup closes it.
When combining Fixed and Stretch columns, generally you only want one, maybe two trailing columns to use _WidthStretch.
When disabling anti-aliasing lines, you'll probably want to disable borders in your style as well.
When docking is enabled, you can ALWAYS dock MOST window into another! Try it now!
When drawing circle primitives with "num_segments == 0" tesselation will be calculated automatically.
When sorting is enabled: allow no sorting, disable default sorting. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount == 0).
When sorting is enabled: hold shift when clicking headers to sort on multiple column. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount > 1).
